msg:At first, I chose Yachen because of the children's playground. It is very suitable for families with children. Compared with other hotels, this kind of children's playground is not perfunctory play. However, they only allow one adult and one child to enter. The other parent can sit on the chair in the restaurant outside and wait. The hotel is right next to Dishui Lake. It is very convenient to cross the road on the first floor.

The hotel is very large, with at least two buildings. It is also very convenient to drive here. There are two floors in the underground parking lot. B1 is a three-dimensional parking garage that can directly reach the hotel lobby front desk. B2 does not have a three-dimensional parking garage and can directly reach the hotel guest room. Yes, the guest room and the front desk are not in the same building.

I checked in at 3 pm on May 2nd. Unfortunately, there were too many people on Labor Day, and the guest room could not be cleaned up at once. After storing the luggage, I took the children to the children's playground to play. It was not until five o'clock that I was notified that I could go to get the room card. The deposit was 1,000 yuan.

The front desk will provide children's toothbrushes and slippers, adult toothbrushes and combs, and a pack of Maltesers. If you drive, remember to scan the code at the front desk to register your vehicle information, so that you can enter and exit the parking lot for free during your stay.

The garden-view king room is 40 square meters, with a large and comfortable space. The drinks in the mini bar refrigerator are free for the first round. Four bottles of mineral water are provided in the room, which can't be finished every day. I also made an appoin**ent to play in the billiard room for an hour. Unfortunately, we didn't bring swimsuits and didn't try the swimming pool.

We tried two restaurants in the hotel, one is the Chinese restaurant on the third floor. We ordered dishes, which are a little expensive but taste good. The other is Chao Coffee on the first floor. There is only a self-service hot pot in the evening, 260 per person, and children under 1.2 meters tall don't need to buy. The buffet breakfast in the morning is quite rich, with many varieties and wide distribution.

There is a second floor here with small and medium-sized slides + climbing frames. You need to change your shoes when entering. The hotel will provide non-slip socks. You cannot eat inside. In addition, when Ctrip bought the tickets, I noticed that there was a stunning VR machine in the park, but unfortunately it was not playable. I hope the hotel can improve this. It can set time and request reservations, but such a great machine is expensive to buy. Yeah, it's really a waste just to put it there.
The room was clean and comfortable, and there were free drinks in the refrigerator on the first day. The cleaners on the floor were also very polite. Overall it is indeed a 5 star standard.
The swimming pool is also a place I like very much. Although it takes a long time to walk, you will also pass through a super empty area without air conditioning. It is very cold there, so if you are bringing a baby, remember to bring an extra towel to wrap the baby securely. There is a massage pool next to the swimming pool. It is comfortable for those who don't know how to swim to get a massage directly with three beds. However, what needs to be improved is that there are no service staff in the locker room. If you want to dry towels, you can't find anyone. After staying for three days, I found that there were quite a lot of people who looked like lifeguards in the swimming pool. It seemed like there were at least three people in one class. However, the service in the locker room was zero. You had to go to the lifeguard on your own to change hands at the front desk. I saw many new ones. The guests who arrived looked confused for a long time. The staff clearly saw the people who were coming to swim through the large glass in the corridor. They did not take the initiative to go out and change their hand cards. They waited for them to come in and ask questions before processing. , I think the service is not good at this point.
The hotel is just across a small road from the lake. If the weather is good, you can go out for a walk. If you have children, go to the right and there is a place where you can borrow cute automatic cars. However, the price is not cheap. It takes 70/30 minutes during the Chinese New Year. There is a small river right outside the buffet side door, and you can set off fireworks on the bridge, which is considered to be outside the scope of the hotel.
Dinner is my favorite. It is very cost-effective and the environment is good. The dishes are very comprehensive. Salmon, hot pot, raw beef, and freshly made tiramisu are all my favorites. I haven't had enough after eating it for two days. There are very few choices of wine buffet. It is recommended to add more varieties. The attitude of the waiters is also very enthusiastic (but during the Chinese New Year, it is obvious that a lot of temporary cleaning ladies have been hired. During breakfast, I saw some shady cleaners. Temporary workers and permanent workers can be distinguished at a glance)
The overall evaluation is that I think it is the most satisfactory choice during the Chinese New Year. The environment is comfortable, the food is delicious, the service is enthusiastic, and the children also have fun. I will come to visit your home during the Chinese New Year next year.

Summary: I think the hotel's catering needs to be improved, otherwise it would be a pity if it doesn't match such good hardware. Small suggestion: Due to geographical reasons, I think most of the guests are locals in Shanghai or families with children vacationing on weekends and holidays, rather than guests traveling to Shanghai from outside. What you want to attract are local repeat customers. The supplies for children should be richer and better, and soft drinks and snacks in the minibar are free. Children will value this very much, and they will even directly link the quality of the hotel to these bottles of drinks. These points can attract repeat vacationers. But the key point is to improve the catering! Nowadays, the basic rooms in InterContinental, Jinjiang and Artychen all cost around 1,000. 1. The room is too hot. At present, the central air conditioner only supports natural wind, and the lowest adjustment is only 23 degrees. Even if I start to open the windows in the afternoon to ventilate, the room still feels very hot after 10 o'clock in the evening. I found an engineer, and the reply to me was that the natural wind of 23 degrees is the best possible effort, and it is completely incomprehensible for fat residents...
2. At around 8 o'clock, the room suddenly tripped, and the TV and all the lights went out. I thought I had won a lottery, even if there was a power outage. Unfortunately, this was quite a drop in price. Quanji and Home Inns had never encountered similar problems.

Ah yes, it's sad without wontons. The waiter will come over professionally and ask you if you want tea or coffee, reflecting the glimmer of a five-star restaurant. The orange juice should be brewed, not freshly squeezed, and the layer of egg fried rice is already in the shape of rice crust. Anyway, not so five-star experience. But in retrospect, the occupancy rate is not very guaranteed, and the restaurant is bound to deduct costs, which is also a helpless move.
Before leaving, the hotel also listened to relevant suggestions and delivered tea (not opened yet). In short, I can feel the efforts of the service, but the helpless move of some hardware can only be said to be forced by the situation. It has not been long since the opening As a result, it has been tossed all the time, and a bunch of facilities can only be suspended first. I hope that the construction of Lingang will get better and better, so that the hotel can play its due level.
